		<div class="g_bubble desc">
<b>Taketatsu Ayana</b> is a voice actress (seiyuu) born on June 23, 1989 in Saitama Prefecture, Japan. She currently belongs to <a href="http://anidb.net/cr32665">Assemble Heart</a> and was formerly affiliated with <a href="http://anidb.net/cr1455">I'm Enterprise</a>. Her blood type is O. She had attended Nihon Narration Engi Kenkyuujo (日本ナレーション演技研究所), a voice actor training school before becoming affiliated with the current management company.
		</div>
